		<div id="primary" class="content-area">
	<div class="content-container site-container">
		<div id="main" class="site-main">
						<div class="content-wrap">
				<article id="post-24997" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-24997 page type-page status-publish hentry grow-content-main grow-content-body">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id24997_fcab2e-42 alignfull has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column24997_a0b488-35"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column24997_c1dce3-a6"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading24997_bde973-4d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading24997_bde973-4d">Immerse <mark class="kt-highlight">yourself in the </mark>local <mark class="kt-highlight">culture for more </mark>meaningful <mark class="kt-highlight">memories</mark></h2>



<p>Tired of the same repeated recommendations from bloggers across the web? Leveraging my fluency in multiple languages, I ignore what other English-language bloggers say and get my intel from local sources (and people, of course). Here, you&#8217;ll find cultural travel guides, food guides, and culture-forward itineraries, especially tailored for us solo female travelers!</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns24997_ff6a38-fe"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn24997_0bb39c-a0 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://polyglotpetra.com/cultural-travel-experience/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Start Planning Your Trip</span></a></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id24997_a1e6be-e5 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column24997_fa1b63-92"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-icon kt-svg-icons kt-svg-icons24997_fcf67a-1e alignnone">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-single-icon kt-svg-style-stacked kt-svg-icon-wrap kt-svg-item-24997_6251ea-25"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_plane-departure"><svg viewBox="0 0 640 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M624 448H16c-8.84 0-16 7.16-16 16v32c0 8.84 7.16 16 16 16h608c8.84 0 16-7.16 16-16v-32c0-8.84-7.16-16-16-16zM80.55 341.27c6.28 6.84 15.1 10.72 24.33 10.71l130.54-.18a65.62 65.62 0 0 0 29.64-7.12l290.96-147.65c26.74-13.57 50.71-32.94 67.02-58.31 18.31-28.48 20.3-49.09 13.07-63.65-7.21-14.57-24.74-25.27-58.25-27.45-29.85-1.94-59.54 5.92-86.28 19.48l-98.51 49.99-218.7-82.06a17.799 17.799 0 0 0-18-1.11L90.62 67.29c-10.67 5.41-13.25 19.65-5.17 28.53l156.22 98.1-103.21 52.38-72.35-36.47a17.804 17.804 0 0 0-16.07.02L9.91 230.22c-10.44 5.3-13.19 19.12-5.57 28.08l76.21 82.97z"/></svg></span></div>
</div>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id24997_620e9a-5c alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column24997_cdd3f0-aa"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p>I don&#8217;t agree with skipping touristy sights. They are touristy for a good reason! But the moments that stayed with me the most from my own trips were from laughing over drinks with my local friends at a bar tourists don&#8217;t go to, or not knowing which bus to take so a local senior woman lent a hand to help. I think it&#8217;s important to mix both these sides of travel for a memorable trip.</p>



<p><strong>I started this blog to help other female travelers balance seeing what they need to see (or else FOMO strikes) and discovering the real local culture. </strong></p>



<p>Every single one of my carefully-researched guides will help you travel with more intention and understanding the cultural context behind what you&#8217;re seeing. That is the only way these memories don&#8217;t fade!</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column24997_10d594-f2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading24997_f1f877-1c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading24997_f1f877-1c">Meet the Author</h2>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading24997_3599f4-12 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading24997_3599f4-12">Petra Udomprasert</h3>



<p>As a digital nomad and perpetual traveler (wanted to say long-term, but it didn&#8217;t feel perpetual enough 😂), I began planning my own trips around what made my own soul swell. Seeing the big cultural sights, balancing that with cultural immersion and discovering the places on a local level.</p>



<p>Now I share those same planning frameworks and mindset here, so you can experience your destinations with the same sense of connection.</p>



<p><a href="https://polyglotpetra.com/about/" data-type="page" data-id="20139">Wondering who I am and how I got here? Read my story!</a></p>
